    <script src="/js/WaitingUserCount.js?1591065522"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript">

        const waitingUserCount = new window.TwScripts.WaitingUserCount.WaitingUserCount(
            'https://frontendapi.twitcasting.tv',
            '825kou'
        );
        var isWaitingUserCountEnabled = true;

        function TwitCastingLiveEventReceived(userid, mid, type, value) {

            if (type == "onlive") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "true");
                window.movieid = mid;
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof hide_related_lives == "function") {
                    hide_related_lives();
                }

                                check_is_collabo_enabled();
                                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.stop();
                }
                return "OK";
            } else if (type === "offline") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "false");
                window.comment_update_interval = 8000;

                if (window.current_frame_id) {
                    window.current_frame_id = 0;
                }

                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof load_related_lives == "function") {
                    load_related_lives();
                }
                                setTimeout(function () {
                    check_is_collabo_enabled();
                }, 3000);
                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.start();
                }
                            } else if (type == "timeup") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-near-timeup", value > 0);
            } else if (type == "item") {
                // Received Items, value = count of items received
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type == "continue") {
                // Received Continue Event
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type === "comment_update_interval") {
                window.comment_update_interval = value;
                if (typeof window.updateCommentUpdateInterval === "function") {
                    window.updateCommentUpdateInterval(parseInt(value, 10));
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

    <script src="/js/WaitingUserCount.js?1591065522"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript">

        const waitingUserCount = new window.TwScripts.WaitingUserCount.WaitingUserCount(
            'https://frontendapi.twitcasting.tv',
            '825kou'
        );
        var isWaitingUserCountEnabled = true;

        function TwitCastingLiveEventReceived(userid, mid, type, value) {

            if (type == "onlive") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "true");
                window.movieid = mid;
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof hide_related_lives == "function") {
                    hide_related_lives();
                }

                                check_is_collabo_enabled();
                                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.stop();
                }
                return "OK";
            } else if (type === "offline") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "false");
                window.comment_update_interval = 8000;

                if (window.current_frame_id) {
                    window.current_frame_id = 0;
                }

                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof load_related_lives == "function") {
                    load_related_lives();
                }
                                setTimeout(function () {
                    check_is_collabo_enabled();
                }, 3000);
                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.start();
                }
                            } else if (type == "timeup") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-near-timeup", value > 0);
            } else if (type == "item") {
                // Received Items, value = count of items received
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type == "continue") {
                // Received Continue Event
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type === "comment_update_interval") {
                window.comment_update_interval = value;
                if (typeof window.updateCommentUpdateInterval === "function") {
                    window.updateCommentUpdateInterval(parseInt(value, 10));
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

    <script src="/js/WaitingUserCount.js?1591065522"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript">

        const waitingUserCount = new window.TwScripts.WaitingUserCount.WaitingUserCount(
            'https://frontendapi.twitcasting.tv',
            '825kou'
        );
        var isWaitingUserCountEnabled = true;

        function TwitCastingLiveEventReceived(userid, mid, type, value) {

            if (type == "onlive") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "true");
                window.movieid = mid;
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof hide_related_lives == "function") {
                    hide_related_lives();
                }

                                check_is_collabo_enabled();
                                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.stop();
                }
                return "OK";
            } else if (type === "offline") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "false");
                window.comment_update_interval = 8000;

                if (window.current_frame_id) {
                    window.current_frame_id = 0;
                }

                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof load_related_lives == "function") {
                    load_related_lives();
                }
                                setTimeout(function () {
                    check_is_collabo_enabled();
                }, 3000);
                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.start();
                }
                            } else if (type == "timeup") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-near-timeup", value > 0);
            } else if (type == "item") {
                // Received Items, value = count of items received
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type == "continue") {
                // Received Continue Event
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type === "comment_update_interval") {
                window.comment_update_interval = value;
                if (typeof window.updateCommentUpdateInterval === "function") {
                    window.updateCommentUpdateInterval(parseInt(value, 10));
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

    <script src="/js/WaitingUserCount.js?1591065522"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript">

        const waitingUserCount = new window.TwScripts.WaitingUserCount.WaitingUserCount(
            'https://frontendapi.twitcasting.tv',
            '825kou'
        );
        var isWaitingUserCountEnabled = true;

        function TwitCastingLiveEventReceived(userid, mid, type, value) {

            if (type == "onlive") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "true");
                window.movieid = mid;
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof hide_related_lives == "function") {
                    hide_related_lives();
                }

                                check_is_collabo_enabled();
                                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.stop();
                }
                return "OK";
            } else if (type === "offline") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "false");
                window.comment_update_interval = 8000;

                if (window.current_frame_id) {
                    window.current_frame_id = 0;
                }

                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof load_related_lives == "function") {
                    load_related_lives();
                }
                                setTimeout(function () {
                    check_is_collabo_enabled();
                }, 3000);
                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.start();
                }
                            } else if (type == "timeup") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-near-timeup", value > 0);
            } else if (type == "item") {
                // Received Items, value = count of items received
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type == "continue") {
                // Received Continue Event
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type === "comment_update_interval") {
                window.comment_update_interval = value;
                if (typeof window.updateCommentUpdateInterval === "function") {
                    window.updateCommentUpdateInterval(parseInt(value, 10));
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

    <script src="/js/WaitingUserCount.js?1591065522"></script>
    <script type="text/javascript">

        const waitingUserCount = new window.TwScripts.WaitingUserCount.WaitingUserCount(
            'https://frontendapi.twitcasting.tv',
            '825kou'
        );
        var isWaitingUserCountEnabled = true;

        function TwitCastingLiveEventReceived(userid, mid, type, value) {

            if (type == "onlive") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "true");
                window.movieid = mid;
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof hide_related_lives == "function") {
                    hide_related_lives();
                }

                                check_is_collabo_enabled();
                                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.stop();
                }
                return "OK";
            } else if (type === "offline") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-is-onlive", "false");
                window.comment_update_interval = 8000;

                if (window.current_frame_id) {
                    window.current_frame_id = 0;
                }

                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
                if (typeof load_related_lives == "function") {
                    load_related_lives();
                }
                                setTimeout(function () {
                    check_is_collabo_enabled();
                }, 3000);
                if(isWaitingUserCountEnabled){
                    waitingUserCount.start();
                }
                            } else if (type == "timeup") {
                document.body.setAttribute("data-near-timeup", value > 0);
            } else if (type == "item") {
                // Received Items, value = count of items received
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type == "continue") {
                // Received Continue Event
                if (typeof updateItems == "function") {
                    updateItems();
                }
            } else if (type === "comment_update_interval") {
                window.comment_update_interval = value;
                if (typeof window.updateCommentUpdateInterval === "function") {
                    window.updateCommentUpdateInterval(parseInt(value, 10));
                }
            }
        }
    </script>
